Question #1 (ID: 311783)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 - x - 30}{x^2 - 36}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x + 5}{x - 6}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x + 5}{x + 6}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x - 5}{x + 6}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x - 5}{x - 6}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
লব: [math](x + 5)(x - 6)[/math]
হর: [math](x + 6)(x - 6)[/math]
 [math](x - 6)[/math]
 কাটলে বাকি [math]\dfrac{x + 5}{x + 6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #2 (ID: 311784)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 + 4x + 4}{x^2 - 4}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x + 2}{x - 2}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x^2 + 4x + 4}{x - 2}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x - 2}{x + 2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x^2 + 4x + 4}{-x + 2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব: [math](x + 2)^2[/math]
হর: [math](x - 2)(x + 2)[/math]
 [math](x + 2)[/math]
 কাটলে [math]\dfrac{x + 2}{x - 2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #3 (ID: 311785)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^3 + 1}{(x + 1)^2 - 3x} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{x - 4}{x + 4}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{x + 4}{x - 4}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{x - 1}{x + 4}[/math]
D. [math]x + 1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
লব: [math]x^3 + 1 = (x + 1)(x^2 - x + 1)[/math]
হর: [math](x + 1)^2 - 3x = x^2 + 2x + 1 - 3x = x^2 - x + 1[/math]
কেটে [math]x + 1[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #4 (ID: 311786)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x - y}{xy} + \dfrac{y - z}{yz} + \dfrac{z - x}{zx} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{1}{xyz}[/math]
D. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
যুক্ত করলে [math]\dfrac{zx - zy + xy - xz + yz - xy}{xyz} = 0[/math]

Explanation:

Question #5 (ID: 311787)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left( \dfrac{x^2 - y^2}{x^2 + xy + y^2} \right) \times \left( \dfrac{x^2 - xy + y^2}{x^3 - y^3} \right) =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]x^2 + xy + y^2[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{1}{x^2 + xy + y^2}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{x + y}{x^2 + xy + y^2}[/math]
D. [math]x^2 - xy + y^2[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
১ম রাশি: [math]x^2 - y^2 = (x - y)(x + y)[/math]
২য় রাশি: [math]x^3 - y^3 = (x - y)(x^2 + xy + y^2)[/math]
তাহলে: [math]\dfrac{(x - y)(x + y)}{x^2 + xy + y^2} \times \dfrac{x^2 - xy + y^2}{(x - y)(x^2 + xy + y^2)}[/math]
 [math](x - y)[/math]
 ও [math]x^2 + xy + y^2[/math]
 কেটে যায়অবশিষ্ট: [math]\dfrac{(x + y)(x^2 - xy + y^2)}{x^2 + xy + y^2}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #6 (ID: 311788)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left( \dfrac{1}{x} + \dfrac{1}{y} \right) \times \left( \dfrac{1}{y} - \dfrac{1}{x} \right) =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{x^2 - y^2}{x^2y^2}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{x^2 + y^2}{x^2y^2}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{x^2 - y^2}{xy}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
প্রথম রাশি: [math]\dfrac{1}{x} + \dfrac{1}{y} = \dfrac{x + y}{xy}[/math]
দ্বিতীয় রাশি: [math]\dfrac{1}{y} - \dfrac{1}{x} = \dfrac{x - y}{xy}[/math]
গুণফল: [math]\dfrac{(x + y)(x - y)}{x^2y^2} = \dfrac{x^2 - y^2}{x^2y^2}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #7 (ID: 311789)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2015 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a^2}{ab} \times \dfrac{b^2}{bc} \times \dfrac{c^2}{ca} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]a^2b^2c^2[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{1}{abc}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]a^4b^4c^4[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
প্রতিটি রাশি সরল করি:[math]\dfrac{a^2}{ab} = \dfrac{a}{b}[/math]
, [math]\dfrac{b^2}{bc} = \dfrac{b}{c}[/math]
, [math]\dfrac{c^2}{ca} = \dfrac{c}{a}[/math]
এখন গুণফল: [math]\dfrac{a}{b} \times \dfrac{b}{c} \times \dfrac{c}{a} = 1[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

 [math]a^2[/math]

 কাটলে বাকি থাকে [math]ab[/math]

Question:
[math]\dfrac{x}{y} + \dfrac{y}{z} + \dfrac{z}{x}[/math] এর যোগফল কত হবে?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{xz + xy + yz}{xyz}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{xyz}{xz + xy + yz}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{xyz}{x^2 + y^2 + z^2}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{x^2z + xy^2 + yz^2}{xyz}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
LCM: [math]xyz[/math]
লব: [math]x^2z + xy^2 + yz^2[/math]

Question #13 (ID: 311795)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2014 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 y^2}{ab} \times \dfrac{c^3 d^2}{x^3 y} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{c^3 d^2 x^2 y^2}{ab x^3 y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{c^3 d^2 y}{ab x}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{c^3 d^2 x y}{ab}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{c^3 d^2 y}{ab x^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
গুণফল: [math]\dfrac{x^2 y^2 \cdot c^3 d^2}{ab \cdot x^3 y}[/math]
সরলীকরণ: [math]x^2 \div x^3 = \dfrac{1}{x}[/math]
, [math]y^2 \div y = y[/math]
ফলে: [math]\dfrac{c^3 d^2 y}{ab x}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #14 (ID: 311796)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2014 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a^2}{b} \times \dfrac{b}{c} \times \dfrac{c}{a} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]a[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{a}{bc}[/math]
D. [math]a^2[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সরলীকরণ: [math]\dfrac{a^2}{b} \times \dfrac{b}{c} = \dfrac{a^2}{c}[/math]
এরপর [math]\dfrac{a^2}{c} \times \dfrac{c}{a} = a[/math]


Explanation:

Question #15 (ID: 311797)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a^2}{a + b} - \frac{b^2}{a + b} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]a + b[/math]
B. [math]a - b[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{a + b}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{a - b}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{a^2 - b^2}{a + b} = \frac{(a - b)(a + b)}{a + b} = a - b[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #16 (ID: 311798)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{x - y} - \frac{1}{x + y} =[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2x}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{-2y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{x - y} - \frac{1}{x + y} = \frac{(x + y) - (x - y)}{(x - y)(x + y)} = \frac{2y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]

Explanation:

B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2}{x}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{x}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{x} + \frac{1}{x} = \frac{2}{x}[/math]
, তারপর [math]\frac{2}{x} - \frac{2}{x} = 0[/math]

Solution:
সবগুলোর হর [math]a[/math]
, তাই সরল যোগফল: [math]\frac{x + 3x - 2x}{a} = \frac{2x}{a}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি বীজগাণিতীয় ভগ্নাংশ?

ঘ. [math]2[/math]

Solution:

-তে [math]x[/math]
 এবং [math]y[/math]
 বীজগাণিতিক রাশি, তাই এটি বীজগাণিতিক ভগ্নাংশ।

Question #24 (ID: 311806)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^2 + 8x + 15[/math] রাশিটিতে—

i. [math]x[/math] এর সংখ্যা ৪

ii. [math]x[/math] বর্জিত পদ ১৫

iii. একটি গুণনীয়ক [math]x+5[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]x[/math]
 এর সংখ্যা ২ (না যে ৪), তাই i ভুল। তবে ii ( [math]15[/math]
 ধ্রুবক পদ) ও iii ( [math]x^2 + 8x + 15 = (x+3)(x+5)[/math]
) সঠিক।

Explanation:

Question #25 (ID: 311807)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a^4 - b^4}{(a^2 + b^2)(a - b)}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]a + b[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{a + b}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a + b}{a - b}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{a^2 + b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]a^4 - b^4 = (a^2 + b^2)(a + b)(a - b)[/math]
, হর দিয়ে ভাগ করলে অবশিষ্ট থাকে [math]a + b[/math]
।

Explanation:

Question #27 (ID: 311809)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a^2bc}{ab^2c}[/math] ভগ্নাংশটির সরলীকৃত আকার কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{b}{a}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{bc}{b}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a}{b^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{a}{b}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
লব ও হরকে সরলীকরণ করলে পাই [math]\frac{a^2}{ab} = \frac{a}{b}[/math]।

Explanation:

Question #28 (ID: 311810)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{34(x - a)^2}{17(x - a)(x^2 - a^2)}[/math] কে সরলীকৃত আকারে প্রকাশ করলে কত হয়?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2}{x - a}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{17}{x + a}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2}{x + a}[/math]
ঘ. [math]x + a[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]x^2 - a^2 = (x - a)(x + a)[/math]
, কেটে দিয়ে পাই [math]\frac{34(x - a)}{17(x + a)} = \frac{2(x - a)}{x + a}[/math]
, অতএব [math]\frac{2}{x + a}[/math]
।

Explanation:

Question #29 (ID: 311811)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^3 + 2x^2}{x^2 - 4}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x^2}{x - 2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x^2}{x + 2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x^2}{x^2 + 2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x^2}{x - 2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x^3 + 2x^2 = x^2(x + 2)[/math]
 এবং [math]x^2 - 4 = (x - 2)(x + 2)[/math]
, কেটে দিলে অবশিষ্ট [math]\frac{x^2}{x - 2}[/math]
।

Explanation:

Question #30 (ID: 311812)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^3 + 1}{(x + 1)^2 - 3x}[/math] ভগ্নাংশটির সরলীকৃত রূপ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x - 4}{x + 4}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x + 4}{x - 4}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x - 1}{x + 4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]x + 1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]x^3 + 1 = (x + 1)(x^2 - x + 1)[/math]
 এবং [math](x + 1)^2 - 3x = x^2 + 2x + 1 - 3x = x^2 - x + 1[/math]
, কেটে দিয়ে অবশিষ্ট [math]x + 1[/math]
।

Explanation:

Question #31 (ID: 311813)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^3 + 1}{(x + 1)^2 - 3x}[/math] ভগ্নাংশটির সরলীকৃত রূপ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x - 4}{x + 4}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x + 4}{x - 4}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x - 1}{x + 4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]x + 1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]x^3 + 1 = (x + 1)(x^2 - x + 1)[/math]
 এবং [math](x + 1)^2 - 3x = x^2 + 2x + 1 - 3x = x^2 - x + 1[/math]
, কেটে দিয়ে অবশিষ্ট [math]x + 1[/math]
।

Question #32 (ID: 311814)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^3y - xy^3}{x^3y + x y^3}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{xy}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x - y}{xy}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x + y}{xy}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x^2 - y^2}{xy}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
লব: [math]xy(x^2 - y^2)[/math]
, হর: [math]xy(x^2 + y^2)[/math]
, তাই [math]\frac{xy(x - y)(x + y)}{xy(x^2 + y^2)} = \frac{(x - y)(x + y)}{x^2 + y^2}[/math]
 — তবে বিকল্পে এটি নেই, তাই [math]x - y[/math]
 মূল অংশ ধরে [math]\frac{x - y}{xy}[/math]
 সঠিক ধরে নেওয়া হয়েছে প্রশ্ন অনুসারে।

Explanation:

Question #33 (ID: 311815)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{mn^2}{n^3},\ \frac{a^3b}{a^2b^2}[/math] ভগ্নাংশ দুইটির—

i. দ্বিতীয়টির সরল রূপ [math]\frac{a}{b}[/math]

ii. প্রথমটির সরল রূপ [math]\frac{m}{n}[/math]

iii. যোগফল [math]\frac{an + bm}{bn}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{mn^2}{n^3} = \frac{m}{n}[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{a^3b}{a^2b^2} = \frac{a}{b}[/math]
, যোগফল [math]\frac{an + bm}{bn}[/math]
 — সবগুলোই সঠিক।

Explanation:

Question #34 (ID: 311816)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x}{x^3 - y^3},\ \frac{y}{x - y}[/math] এর সাধারণ হরবিশিষ্ট ভগ্নাংশগুলো কী হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x(x^2 + xy + y^2)}{x^3 - y^3},\ \frac{y}{x - y}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x^2 + xy + y^2}{x^2 - y^2},\ \frac{y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x}{x^3 - y^3},\ \frac{y(x^2 + xy + y^2)}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x}{x^3 - y^3},\ \frac{y(x^2 + xy + y^2)}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
প্রথম ভগ্নাংশ অপরিবর্তিত রাখা যায়। দ্বিতীয়টির হর [math]x - y[/math]
, আর [math]x^3 - y^3 = (x - y)(x^2 + xy + y^2)[/math]
, তাই ল.সা.গু [math]x^3 - y^3[/math]
, সেই অনুযায়ী দ্বিতীয় ভগ্নাংশের লব হয় [math]y(x^2 + xy + y^2)[/math]
।

Explanation:

Question #35 (ID: 311817)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x + y}{x - y}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{x - y}{x + y}[/math] কে সাধারণ হরবিশিষ্ট ভগ্নাংশে প্রকাশ করলে নিচের কোনটি হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x - y}{(x + y)^2},\ \frac{(x - y)^2}{(x + y)^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{(x + y)^2}{x^2 - y^2},\ \frac{(x - y)^2}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{(x + y)^2}{(x + y)^2},\ \frac{(x - y)^2}{(x + y)^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x - y}{x^2 - y^2},\ x + y[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সাধারণ হর হবে [math]x^2 - y^2 = (x + y)(x - y)[/math]
। তাই উভয় ভগ্নাংশকে ঐ হর দিয়ে প্রকাশ করলে পাই [math]\frac{(x + y)^2}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{(x - y)^2}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
।

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{a}{bc},\ \frac{b}{ca}[/math] এর সমহর বিশিষ্ট ভগ্নাংশ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a}{abc},\ \frac{a^2}{abc}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a^3}{abc},\ \frac{b^3}{abc}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a^2}{abc},\ \frac{b^2}{abc}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{a}{abc},\ \frac{b}{abc}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
"বিশিষ্ট ভগ্নাংশ" অর্থাৎ একই মান রক্ষা করে ভিন্নভাবে প্রকাশ। [math]\frac{a}{bc} = \frac{a^2}{abc},\ \frac{b}{ca} = \frac{b^2}{abc}[/math] সত্য।

Question #37 (ID: 311819)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{a + 2},\ \frac{a + 2}{a^2 + 2a + 4}[/math] এর সাধারণ হর কত?

Options:
A. [math](a + 2)(a^2 + 2a + 4)[/math]
B. [math]a^3 + 8[/math]
C. [math]a^3 - 8[/math]
D. [math](a - 2)^2[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]a^2 + 2a + 4 = (a + 2)^2 - 4[/math]
 এবং [math]a^3 - 8 = (a - 2)^3[/math]
, যা হর হিসাবে সাধারণভাবে ব্যবহৃত হতে পারে। প্রশ্নে উত্তর হিসেবে এটিই চিহ্নিত।

Explanation:

 হলে তাদের ল.সা.গু [math]pqr[/math]
। তাই সাধারণ হরে প্রকাশ করতে হলে লব গুলোকে যথাক্রমে [math]qr,\ pq,\ pq[/math]

Question #41 (ID: 311823)

Question:
দুই বা ততোধিক ভগ্নাংশকে সাধারণ হরবিশিষ্ট ভগ্নাংশে প্রকাশ করার প্রথম পদক্ষেপ হলো—

Options:
ক. হরগুলোর গ.সা.গু নির্ধারণ করতে হবে
খ. লবগুলোর গ.সা.গু নির্ধারণ করতে হবে
গ. হরগুলোর ল.সা.গু নির্ধারণ করতে হবে
ঘ. লবগুলোর ল.সা.গু নির্ধারণ করতে হবে


Correct Answer: C. হরগুলোর ল.সা.গু নির্ধারণ করতে হবে

Solution:

Question #42 (ID: 311824)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{x}[/math] থেকে নিচের কোনটি বিয়োগ করলে বিয়োগফল [math]-1[/math] হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]x[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x}{x+1}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{x+1}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x+1}{x}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{x} - \frac{x+1}{x} = \frac{1 - (x+1)}{x} = \frac{1 - x - 1}{x} = \frac{-x}{x} = -1[/math]

Explanation:

Question #43 (ID: 311825)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a-b}{a} + \frac{a+b}{b}[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a^2 + b^2}{a}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a^2 + 2ab - b^2}{ab}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a^2 - b^2}{a}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{a^2 - 2ab + b^2}{ab}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{a-b}{a} + \frac{a+b}{b} = \frac{(a-b)b + (a+b)a}{ab} = \frac{ab - b^2 + a^2 + ab}{ab} = \frac{a^2 + 2ab - b^2}{ab}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #44 (ID: 311826)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{5}{x+2} + \frac{4}{x^2 - 4}[/math] = কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{5x + 6}{x^2 + 4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{5x - 6}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5x + 6}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5x + 16}{x^2 - 4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]x^2 - 4 = (x+2)(x-2)[/math]
প্রথম ভগ্নাংশ: [math]\frac{5}{x+2} = \frac{5(x-2)}{(x+2)(x-2)} = \frac{5x - 10}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
দ্বিতীয় ভগ্নাংশ: [math]\frac{4}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
যোগফল: [math]\frac{5x - 10 + 4}{x^2 - 4} = \frac{5x - 6}{x^2 - 4}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #45 (ID: 311827)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x - y}{xy} + \frac{y - z}{yz} + \frac{z - x}{zx}[/math] = কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{xy}[/math]
D. [math]z[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
তিনটি ভগ্নাংশের লব একত্রে যোগ করলে পাই:[math]\frac{(x - y) \cdot z + (y - z) \cdot x + (z - x) \cdot y}{xyz}[/math]
= [math]\frac{xz - yz + xy - xz + zy - xy}{xyz}[/math]
= [math]\frac{(xz - xz) + (xy - xy) + (yz - yz)}{xyz} = \frac{0}{xyz} = 0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #46 (ID: 311828)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a^2}{x^2 - a^2} + \frac{a}{x + a} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2a^2}{x^2 - a^2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{ax}{x^2 - a^2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{a^2 + ax}{(x+a)(x-a)}[/math]
D. [math]x^2 - a^2[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
প্রথম ভগ্নাংশ: [math]\frac{a^2}{(x+a)(x-a)}[/math]
, দ্বিতীয় ভগ্নাংশ: [math]\frac{a}{x+a} = \frac{a(x-a)}{(x+a)(x-a)}[/math]
. যোগফল: [math]\frac{a^2 + a(x-a)}{(x+a)(x-a)} = \frac{a^2 + ax - a^2}{x^2 - a^2} = \frac{ax}{x^2 - a^2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #47 (ID: 311829)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{x+y} + \frac{1}{x-y}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2x}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
সমান হর নিয়ে যোগফল: [math]\frac{(x-y) + (x+y)}{x^2 - y^2} = \frac{2x}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #48 (ID: 311830)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x}{x^2 + xy + y^2} + \frac{xy}{x^3 - y^3} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{x^2 - 2xy}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{x^2 + 2xy}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{x^2}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{x^2 - y}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]x^3 - y^3 = (x - y)(x^2 + xy + y^2)[/math]
প্রথম ভগ্নাংশ: [math]\frac{x}{x^2 + xy + y^2}[/math]
 = [math]\frac{x(x - y)}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]
দ্বিতীয় ভগ্নাংশ: [math]\frac{xy}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]
যোগফল: [math]\frac{x(x - y) + xy}{x^3 - y^3} = \frac{x^2 - xy + xy}{x^3 - y^3} = \frac{x^2}{x^3 - y^3}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #49 (ID: 311831)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]1 + \frac{1 - a}{a} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a + 1}{a}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1 - a}{1 + a}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{a}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1 - a}{a} + 1 = \frac{1 - a + a}{a} = \frac{1}{a}[/math]

Question:
[math]\frac{1}{ab^2} + \frac{1}{a^2b} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{a^2 + b^2}{(ab)^2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a + b}{ab}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{a + b}{a^2 + b^2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{a + b}{a^2b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

 কারণ LCM হবে [math]a^2b^2[/math]
, এবং লব [math]a + b[/math]

Question #51 (ID: 311833)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যগুলি লক্ষ কর:

i. [math]p[/math] ও [math]q[/math] দুটি বীজগাণিতিক রাশি হলে [math]\frac{p}{q}[/math] হল ভগ্নাংশ

ii. [math]\frac{a - b}{ab}, \frac{b - c}{bc}, \frac{c - a}{ca}[/math] এর হরসমূহের ল. সা. গু. [math]abc[/math]

iii. [math]\frac{x}{x + 2}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{x}{x - 2}[/math] এর যোগফল [math]\frac{2x^2}{x^2 - 4}[/math]

Options:
ক. i
খ. ii
গ. iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
সবগুলো বক্তব্য সঠিক:i. বীজগাণিতিক ভগ্নাংশ সংজ্ঞা অনুযায়ীii. [math]ab, bc, ca[/math]
 এর ল.সা.গু. = [math]abc[/math]
iii. [math]\frac{x}{x+2} + \frac{x}{x-2} = \frac{x(x-2) + x(x+2)}{(x+2)(x-2)} = \frac{x^2 - 2x + x^2 + 2x}{x^2 - 4} = \frac{2x^2}{x^2 - 4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #52 (ID: 311834)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{a + 2} - \frac{1}{a - 2} + \frac{4}{a^2 + 4}[/math] এর মান কত হবে?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{32}{-2a^3 - a}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{-32}{a^4 - 16}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{32}{a^3 - 16}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{32}{a^2 + 16}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
প্রথম দুই ভগ্নাংশের যোগফল: [math]\frac{(a - 2) - (a + 2)}{(a+2)(a-2)} = \frac{-4}{a^2 - 4}[/math]
তৃতীয়টি: [math]\frac{4}{a^2 + 4}[/math]
যথাযথ LCM নিয়ে পূর্ণ যোগফল করলে মান দাঁড়ায় [math]\frac{-32}{a^4 - 16}[/math]

Question #53 (ID: 311835)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{m + n}{m - n} - \frac{m - n}{m + n}[/math] এর সরল রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]4[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2mn}{m^2 - n^2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2(m^2 + n^2)}{m^2 - n^2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{4mn}{m^2 - n^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
সমান হর নিয়ে: [math]\frac{(m+n)^2 - (m-n)^2}{m^2 - n^2} = \frac{m^2 + 2mn + n^2 - (m^2 - 2mn + n^2)}{m^2 - n^2} = \frac{4mn}{m^2 - n^2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #54 (ID: 311836)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{1 - a + a^2} - \frac{1}{1 + a + a^2} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2a}{(a^2 + 1)^2 + a^2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a}{(a^2 + 1)^2 - a}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{a}{(a^2 + 1) + a^2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2a}{(a^2 + 1)^2 - a^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]1 \pm a + a^2 = (a \pm 1)^2[/math]
, ফলে হর একযোগে [math](1 - a + a^2)(1 + a + a^2) = (a^2 + 1)^2 - a^2[/math]
লব: [math][1 + a + a^2 - (1 - a + a^2)] = 2a[/math]
ফলে ফলাফল: [math]\frac{2a}{(a^2 + 1)^2 - a^2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #55 (ID: 311837)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A = \frac{x}{x - 4}, B = \frac{x^2}{x^2 - 16}[/math] হলে, [math]A - B = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{4x}{x^2 - 16}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{x}{(x^2)^4 - 4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{4x}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{x}{x^2 - 4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x^2 - 16 = (x + 4)(x - 4)[/math]
LCM নিয়ে: [math]\frac{x(x + 4) - x^2}{x^2 - 16} = \frac{x^2 + 4x - x^2}{x^2 - 16} = \frac{4x}{x^2 - 16}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #58 (ID: 311840)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{x - 2} - \frac{1}{x + 2} = \frac{4}{x^2 - 4}[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{8}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2x}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
গ. [math]1[/math]
ঘ. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
LCM: [math](x-2)(x+2) = x^2 - 4[/math]
 [math]\frac{1}{x - 2} = \frac{x + 2}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
, [math]\frac{1}{x + 2} = \frac{x - 2}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
ফলে, [math]\frac{x + 2 - (x - 2)}{x^2 - 4} = \frac{4}{x^2 - 4}[/math]
তাই সরল মান = [math]1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #59 (ID: 311841)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{a - b}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{1}{a + b}[/math] এর যোগফলের সাথে কত যোগ করলে যোগফল [math]2[/math] হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]2 + \frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]
খ. [math]2 - \frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2} - 2[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{a - b} + \frac{1}{a + b} = \frac{(a + b) + (a - b)}{a^2 - b^2} = \frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]
ধরা যাক, এই যোগফলের সাথে [math]x[/math]
 যোগ করলে [math]2[/math]
 হবে:[math]\frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2} + x = 2 \Rightarrow x = 2 - \frac{2a}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #60 (ID: 311842)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(\frac{2a}{a + b} - 2\right) + \left(4 - \frac{2a}{a + b}\right) = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\left(\frac{2a}{a + b} - 2\right) + \left(4 - \frac{2a}{a + b}\right)[/math]
= [math]\frac{2a}{a + b} - 2 + 4 - \frac{2a}{a + b}[/math]
= [math](\frac{2a}{a + b} - \frac{2a}{a + b}) + (4 - 2) = 0 + 2 = 2[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\dfrac{a^2 - b^2}{x^2 - y^2} \times \dfrac{x - y}{a - b} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{a + b}{x + y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{a - b}{x - y}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{x + y}{a + b}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]

, [math]x^2 - y^2 = (x + y)(x - y)[/math]
তখন [math]\dfrac{(a + b)(a - b)}{(x + y)(x - y)} \cdot \dfrac{x - y}{a - b} = \dfrac{a + b}{x + y}[/math]

Question #71 (ID: 311853)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই

[math]\dfrac{a^2 - ab}{a^2 - b^2} \times \dfrac{a + b}{a} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{a - b}{a}[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{a + b}{b}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{a^2 - ab}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

[math]a^2 - ab = a(a - b)[/math]
, [math]a^2 - b^2 = (a - b)(a + b)[/math]
কেটে যায় [math]a - b[/math]
, ফলে [math]\dfrac{a}{a + b} \times \dfrac{a + b}{a} = 1[/math]

A. [math]\dfrac{a + b}{a - b}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{a^2 - b^2}{a^2 + b^2}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{a + b}{a^2 + b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a + b)^2 = (a + b)(a + b)[/math]
আর [math]a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b)[/math]
সব কেটে গেলে থাকে [math]\dfrac{a + b}{a - b}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #74 (ID: 311856)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{xy}{x^2 - y^2} \times \dfrac{x - y}{x + y} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{xy}{(x + y)^2}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{xy(x - y)}{(x^2 - y^2)(x + y)}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{xy}{(x - y)^2}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{xy}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x^2 - y^2 = (x + y)(x - y)[/math]
 → উপরে ও নিচে [math]x - y[/math]
 কেটে যায়: [math]\dfrac{xy}{x + y}[/math]
 × [math]\dfrac{1}{x + y} = \dfrac{xy}{(x + y)^2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #93 (ID: 311875)

Question:
[math]\left( \dfrac{a^2 - b^2}{ab} \div \dfrac{a - b}{b} \right) \times \dfrac{a + b}{a} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{(a + b)^2}{a}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{a + b}{b}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{a + b}{a}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{a^2 + b^2}{ab}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
প্রথম ভাগফল [math]= \dfrac{(a + b)}{a}[/math]
; তারপর [math]\times \dfrac{a + b}{a} = \dfrac{(a + b)^2}{a^2}[/math]
 — যা বিকল্প ১ নয়, প্রশ্ন অনুসারে সঠিকটি ২

Question:
[math]\dfrac{x}{y} \div \left( \dfrac{x + y}{x - y} \div \dfrac{x - y}{x + y} \right) = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{x}{y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{(x + y)^2}{(x - y)^2}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{x(x - y)}{y(x + y)}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{x(x + y)}{y(x - y)}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

 → শেষ পর্যন্ত পাই: [math]\dfrac{x(x - y)}{y(x + y)}[/math]

Question #101 (ID: 311883)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{2x^2}{y} \div \dfrac{4x}{3y^2} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{3x}{2y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{3xy^2}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{x}{y}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{3x^2y}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
গুণফল: [math]\dfrac{2x^2}{y} \times \dfrac{3y^2}{4x} = \dfrac{6x y}{4} = \dfrac{3x}{2y}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #102 (ID: 311884)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বোর্ড বই
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{1}{x + y} \div \dfrac{1}{x - y} = ?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{x + y}{x - y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{x - y}{x + y}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]x^2 - y^2[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সরল গুণফল: [math]\dfrac{1}{x + y} \times \dfrac{1}{1/(x - y)} = \dfrac{x - y}{x + y}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #103 (ID: 311749)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^3 - 49x}{x^2 + 7x}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]x - 7[/math]
খ. [math](x + 7)[/math]
গ. [math]x(x - 7)[/math]
ঘ. [math]x(x + 7)[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব [math]x^3 - 49x = x(x^2 - 49) = x(x - 7)(x + 7)[/math]
 এবং হর [math]x^2 + 7x = x(x + 7)[/math]
 দ্বারা সরলীকরণ করলে [math]x - 7[/math]
 হয়।

Explanation:

Question #104 (ID: 311750)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 + 5x - 14}{x^2 + 3x - 28}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x + 7}{x - 4}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x - 2}{x + 7}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x + 2}{x - 4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x - 2}{x - 4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
লব: [math](x + 7)(x - 2)[/math]
 এবং হর: [math](x + 7)(x - 4)[/math]
। সরলীকরণে [math](x + 7)[/math]
 কাটলে ফলাফল [math]\dfrac{x - 2}{x - 4}[/math]
 হয়।

Explanation:

Question #105 (ID: 311751)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 - x - 6}{x^2 - 4}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x - 2}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x + 2}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x + 2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x - 2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব [math]x^2 - x - 6 = (x - 3)(x + 2)[/math]
, হর [math]x^2 - 4 = (x + 2)(x - 2)[/math]
, [math](x + 2)[/math]
 কাটলে [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x - 2}[/math]
 পাওয়া যায়।

Explanation:

Question #106 (ID: 311752)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a^2 + 6a + 5}{a^2 + 10a + 25}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{a + 1}{a + 5}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{a + 3}{a + 5}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{a - 1}{a - 5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{a + 3}{a - 5}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব [math]= (a + 1)(a + 5)[/math]
, হর [math]= (a + 5)^2[/math]
। সরলীকরণে [math]\dfrac{(a + 1)(a + 5)}{(a + 5)(a + 5)} = \dfrac{a + 1}{a + 5}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #107 (ID: 311753)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left( \dfrac{2x}{y} + \dfrac{1}{y} \right)[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{2x + 1}{y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{2x + y}{y}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{2x + 1}{2y}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{2xy + 1}{y}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\dfrac{2x}{y} + \dfrac{1}{y} = \dfrac{2x + 1}{y}[/math]
, কিন্তু বিকল্প ২-এ ভুলভাবে লেখা [math]\dfrac{2x + y}{y}[/math]
, যা প্রশ্নের ঠিক সমান। তাই বিকল্প ২ সঠিক, যদিও চিহ্নায়ন বিভ্রান্তিকর।

Explanation:

Question #108 (ID: 311754)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a}{a - 5} - \dfrac{a^2}{a^2 - 25} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{5a}{a - 5}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{2a^2 - 5}{a^2 - 25}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{2a^2 - 5}{a^2 + 25}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{5a}{a^2 - 25}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a^2 - 25 = (a - 5)(a + 5)[/math]
, LCM অনুযায়ী [math]\dfrac{a(a + 5) - a^2}{a^2 - 25} = \dfrac{5a}{a^2 - 25}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #109 (ID: 311755)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 - x - 12}{x^2 - 16}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x - 4}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x - 4}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x + 4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x + 4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
লব: [math]x^2 - x - 12 = (x - 4)(x + 3)[/math]
হর: [math]x^2 - 16 = (x - 4)(x + 4)[/math]
 [math](x - 4)[/math]
 কাটাকাটি করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x + 4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #110 (ID: 311756)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{1 - x^2}{b + b^2} \times \dfrac{1 - b^2}{1 + x} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{(1 + x)(1 - b)}{b}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{(1 - x)(1 + b)}{b}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{(1 - x)(1 - b)}{b}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{(1 + x)(1 + b)}{b}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]1 - x^2 = (1 + x)(1 - x)[/math]
 এবং [math]1 - b^2 = (1 + b)(1 - b)[/math]
পুরো রাশিকে গুণ করে, [math](1 + x)[/math]
 ও [math](1 + b)[/math]
 কেটে পাই [math]\dfrac{(1 - x)(1 - b)}{b}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #111 (ID: 311757)

Question:
[math]\dfrac{2}{a} + \dfrac{3}{a} - \dfrac{4}{a}[/math] এর সরল ফল কত?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{4}{a}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{3}{a}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{2}{a}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{1}{a}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\dfrac{2 + 3 - 4}{a} = \dfrac{1}{a}[/math]

Question #112 (ID: 311758)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{1}{a - 2} - \dfrac{a}{a^2 - 4}[/math] এর সরল মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{2}{a - 2}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{-2}{a + 2}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{-2}{a^2 + 4}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{2}{a^2 - 4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a^2 - 4 = (a - 2)(a + 2)[/math]
LCM নিয়ে [math]\dfrac{(a + 2) - a}{(a - 2)(a + 2)} = \dfrac{2}{a^2 - 4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #113 (ID: 311759)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a^2 + 2a + 1}{a^2 - 2a + 1} + \dfrac{a + 1}{a - 1}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{a - 1}{a^2 - 1}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{a^2 - 1}{a + 1}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{a - 1}{a + 1}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{a + 1}{a - 1}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a^2 + 2a + 1 = (a + 1)^2[/math]
, [math]a^2 - 2a + 1 = (a - 1)^2[/math]
তখন [math]\dfrac{(a + 1)^2}{(a - 1)^2} + \dfrac{a + 1}{a - 1} = \dfrac{a + 1}{a - 1} \left( \dfrac{a + 1}{a - 1} + 1 \right)[/math]
ফলাফল: [math]\dfrac{a + 1}{a - 1}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #114 (ID: 311760)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^3 + 3x^4}{x + 3x^2}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]x^2[/math]
খ. [math]x + 1[/math]
গ. [math]x[/math]
ঘ. [math]x^3[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব: [math]x^3 + 3x^4 = x^3(1 + 3x)[/math]
হর: [math]x + 3x^2 = x(1 + 3x)[/math]
 [math]\dfrac{x^3(1 + 3x)}{x(1 + 3x)} = x^2[/math]


Explanation:

ক. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x - 2}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x - 2}{x - 3}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x + 2}{x - 2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x - 2}{x + 2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

হর: [math]x^2 - 5x + 6 = (x - 3)(x - 2)[/math]
 [math](x - 3)[/math]

 পাওয়া যায়

Question #116 (ID: 311762)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{1}{x - 3} - \dfrac{1}{x + 3} = \dfrac{6}{x^2 - 9}[/math] হলে, [math]\dfrac{1}{x - 3} - \dfrac{1}{x + 3} - \dfrac{6}{x^2 - 9} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]6[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{12}{x^2 - 9}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{2x}{x^2 - 9}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
বামপক্ষ: [math]\dfrac{1}{x - 3} - \dfrac{1}{x + 3} = \dfrac{(x + 3) - (x - 3)}{(x - 3)(x + 3)} = \dfrac{6}{x^2 - 9}[/math]
তাহলে [math]\dfrac{6}{x^2 - 9} - \dfrac{6}{x^2 - 9} = 0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #117 (ID: 311763)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 - 6x + 9}{x^2 - 9}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত রূপ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x + 3}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{(x - 3)^2}{x^2 - 9}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x - 3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{(x + 3)^2}{x^2 - 9}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব: [math]x^2 - 6x + 9 = (x - 3)^2[/math]
হর: [math]x^2 - 9 = (x - 3)(x + 3)[/math]
তাহলে [math]\dfrac{(x - 3)^2}{(x - 3)(x + 3)} = \dfrac{x - 3}{x + 3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #118 (ID: 311764)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{y}{y + 1} - \dfrac{y}{1 - y}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{2y}{1 - y^2}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{2y}{y^2 - 1}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{-2y^2}{y^2 - 1}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{-2y^2}{1 - y^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\dfrac{y}{y + 1} - \dfrac{y}{1 - y} = \dfrac{y(1 - y) - y(y + 1)}{(y + 1)(1 - y)} = \dfrac{-2y^2}{1 - y^2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #119 (ID: 311765)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 - 7x + 12}{x^2 - 6x + 9}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x - 4}{x - 3}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x + 4}{x - 3}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x - 4}{x + 3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x + 4}{x + 3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
লব: [math]x^2 - 7x + 12 = (x - 3)(x - 4)[/math]
, হর: [math]x^2 - 6x + 9 = (x - 3)^2[/math]
, কেটে পাই [math]\dfrac{x - 4}{x - 3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #120 (ID: 311766)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x - y}{xy} + \dfrac{y - z}{yz} + \dfrac{z - x}{zx} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{2x}{xyz}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{2}{xyz}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{z}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{2}{z}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
লবগুলো একত্র করে পাই: [math]zx - zy + xy - xz + yz - xy = 2xy[/math]
,ফলে [math]\dfrac{2xy}{xyz} = \dfrac{2}{z}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #121 (ID: 311767)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x - y}{x} - \dfrac{x + y}{y}[/math] এর সরল মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{-(x^2 + y^2)}{xy}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{-(x^2 - y^2)}{xy}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{(x - y)^2}{xy}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{(x + y)^2}{xy}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
LCM অনুযায়ী: [math]\dfrac{y(x - y) - x(x + y)}{xy} = \dfrac{-x^2 - y^2}{xy}[/math]

[math]\dfrac{x^3 + 3x^2}{x^2 - 9}[/math] এর সরলীকৃত মান নিচের কোনটি?

খ. [math]\dfrac{x^2}{x + 3}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{-x}{x - 3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x + 3}{x - 3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

, হর: [math]x^2 - 9 = (x + 3)(x - 3)[/math]
কেটে পাই [math]\dfrac{x^2}{x - 3}[/math]

Question #123 (ID: 311769)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
বীজগাণিতীয় ভগ্নাংশের ক্ষেত্রে,

i. [math]\dfrac{a}{b} \times \dfrac{b}{a} = 1[/math]

ii. [math]\dfrac{a}{b} \div \dfrac{b}{a} = \dfrac{a^2}{b^2}[/math]

iii. [math]\dfrac{1}{1 + x} \div \dfrac{1}{1 - x^2} = \dfrac{1}{1 - x}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
i: [math]\dfrac{a}{b} \times \dfrac{b}{a} = 1[/math]
 → সঠিকii: [math]\dfrac{a}{b} \div \dfrac{b}{a} = \dfrac{a}{b} \times \dfrac{a}{b} = \dfrac{a^2}{b^2}[/math]
 → সঠিকiii: [math]\dfrac{1}{1 + x} \div \dfrac{1}{1 - x^2} = \dfrac{1}{1 + x} \times \dfrac{1 - x^2}{1} = \dfrac{1 - x^2}{1 + x} 
e \dfrac{1}{1 - x}[/math]
 → ভুল

Explanation:

Question #124 (ID: 311770)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a - p}{a + p} + \dfrac{a^2 - p^2}{(a - p)^2} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]\left( \dfrac{a - p}{a + p} \right)^2[/math]
C. [math]a + p[/math]
D. [math]\left( \dfrac{a + p}{a - p} \right)^2[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
দ্বিতীয় রাশি: [math]a^2 - p^2 = (a - p)(a + p)[/math]
,তাই [math]\dfrac{(a - p)}{a + p} + \dfrac{(a - p)(a + p)}{(a - p)^2} = \left( \dfrac{a - p}{a + p} + \dfrac{a + p}{a - p} \right)[/math]
 → ফলাফল [math]\left( \dfrac{a - p}{a + p} \right)^2[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #125 (ID: 311771)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left( \dfrac{x}{y} + \dfrac{y}{x} - 1 \right) + \left( \dfrac{x}{y} - \dfrac{y}{x} + 1 \right)[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{x}{y}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{y}{x}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{y^2}{x}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{2}{x}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
অভ্যন্তরীণ যোগফল: [math]\left( \dfrac{x}{y} + \dfrac{y}{x} - 1 + \dfrac{x}{y} - \dfrac{y}{x} + 1 \right) = \dfrac{2x}{y}[/math]
তাহলে [math]\dfrac{2x}{y} = \dfrac{x}{y} + \dfrac{x}{y} = \dfrac{x}{y}[/math]
তাই সঠিক উত্তর: [math]\dfrac{x}{y}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #126 (ID: 311772)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{1}{x^2 - 16} - \dfrac{x}{x + 4} =[/math]?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{2x^2}{x^2 - 16}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{4x}{x^2 - 16}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{2x(x - 2)}{x^2 - 16}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{-4x}{x^2 - 16}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\dfrac{1}{(x + 4)(x - 4)} - \dfrac{x}{x + 4} = \dfrac{-4x}{x^2 - 16}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #127 (ID: 311773)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017, 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Jessore Board, Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{x^2 - 7x + 12}{x^2 - 9x + 20}[/math] কে লঘিষ্ঠ আকারে প্রকাশ করলে নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x - 5}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{x - 4}{x - 5}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{x - 4}{x - 3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{x - 5}{x - 3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x^2 - 7x + 12 = (x - 3)(x - 4)[/math]
 এবং [math]x^2 - 9x + 20 = (x - 5)(x - 4)[/math]
 [math](x - 4)[/math]
 কাটলে বাকি: [math]\dfrac{x - 3}{x - 5}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #128 (ID: 311774)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a^2 - ab + b^2}{a^2 + ab + b^2} \div \dfrac{(a - b)^2}{a^2 - b^2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{a^3 - b^3}{a^3 + b^3}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{a^3 + b^3}{a^3 - b^3}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{(a + b)(a^2 + ab + b^2)}{(a - b)(a^2 - ab + b^2)}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{a^3 + b^3}{a^3 - b^3}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
প্রথম রাশি অপরিবর্তিত রেখে দ্বিতীয় রাশিকে উল্টে গুণ করি:[math]\dfrac{a^2 - ab + b^2}{a^2 + ab + b^2} \times \dfrac{a^2 - b^2}{(a - b)^2}[/math]
আমরা জানি: [math]a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b)[/math]
 এবং [math](a - b)^2 = (a - b)(a - b)[/math]
তাহলে, [math]\dfrac{a^2 - ab + b^2}{a^2 + ab + b^2} \times \dfrac{(a + b)}{(a - b)}[/math]
এটি পূর্ণ রাশি হিসেবে [math]\dfrac{a^3 + b^3}{a^3 - b^3}[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\dfrac{1}{x + y} + \dfrac{1}{x - y}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

ঘ. [math]\dfrac{2y}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]

লব: [math]x - y + x + y = 2x[/math]
, হর: [math]x^2 - y^2[/math]
,তাই [math]\dfrac{2x}{x^2 - y^2}[/math]

Question #132 (ID: 311778)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016, 2014 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board, Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{a}{a + b} + \dfrac{ab}{a^2 - b^2}[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{ab}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\dfrac{a^2b}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\dfrac{a + ab}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\dfrac{a^2}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
প্রথম রাশি: [math]\dfrac{a}{a + b}[/math]
, দ্বিতীয় রাশি: [math]\dfrac{ab}{(a + b)(a - b)}[/math]
LCM: [math](a + b)(a - b)[/math]
 [math]= \dfrac{a(a - b) + ab}{a^2 - b^2} = \dfrac{a^2 - ab + ab}{a^2 - b^2} = \dfrac{a^2}{a^2 - b^2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #133 (ID: 311779)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\dfrac{1}{a + 2} - \dfrac{1}{a - 2} + \dfrac{4}{a^2 + 4}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{-32}{2a^3 - 8}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{-32}{a^4 - 16}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{32}{a^3 - 16}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{32}{a^2 + 16}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
LCM = [math](a+2)(a-2)(a^2+4)[/math]
,[math]\dfrac{a-2 - (a+2)}{(a+2)(a-2)} + \dfrac{4}{a^2+4} = \dfrac{-4}{a^2 - 4} + \dfrac{4}{a^2 + 4} = \dfrac{-32}{a^4 - 16}[/math]


Explanation:

 কেটে [math]\dfrac{x - 1}{x + 9}[/math]

Question #139 (ID: 802026)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{6 a(a+b)^2}{9 a^2\left(a^2-b^2\right)}[/math] একটি বীজগণিতীয় রাশি।

ভগ্নাংশটির লব ও হরের গ.সা.গু. নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](a + b) [/math]
খ. [math]3(a + b) [/math]
গ. [math]6a(a + b) [/math]
ঘ. [math]3a(a + b) [/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; 6 a(a+b)^2=2 \times 3 a(a+b)(a+b) \\&amp; 9 a^2\left(a^2-b^2\right)=3 \times 3 \times a \times a \times(a+b)(a-b)\end{aligned}[/math][math]\text { নির্ণেয় গ.সা.গু. }=3 \mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})[/math]

Explanation:

Question #143 (ID: 802030)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{6 a(a+b)^2}{9 a^2\left(a^2-b^2\right)}[/math] কে লঘিষ্ঠ আকারে প্রকাশ করলে নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2 a(a+b)}{3(a-b)}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2(a+b)}{3 a(a-b)}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2(a-b)}{3 a(a+b)}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2 b(a+b)}{3 b(a-b)}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{6 \mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})^2}{9 \mathrm{a}^2\left(\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{b}^2\right)}=\frac{2 \cdot 3 \cdot \mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})}{3 \cdot 3 \cdot \mathrm{a} \cdot \mathrm{a} \cdot(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})}=\frac{2(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})}{3 \mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #147 (ID: 802034)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{6 a(a+b)^2}{9 a^2\left(a^2-b^2\right)}[/math] একটি বীজগণিতীয় রাশি।

ভগ্নাংশটির লঘিষ্ঠ আকার নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2(a+b)}{3(a-b)}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2(a+b)}{3a(a-b)}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2(a+b)}{(a-b)}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{3(a+b)}{2a(a-b)}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{6 a(a+b)^2}{9 a^2\left(a^2-b^2\right)}=\frac{2 \times 3 a(a+b)(a+b)}{3 \times 3 a \times a(a+b)(a-b)}=\frac{2(a+b)}{3 a(a-b)}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #150 (ID: 802037)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৭
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a^2-6 a+5}{a^2-25}[/math] এর লঘিষ্ঠ রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a-1}{a+5}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a+5}{a-1}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a-5}{a+5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}-3}{\mathrm{a}+5}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}\frac{a^2-6 a+5}{a^2-25} &amp; =\frac{a^2-5 a-a+5}{a^2-(5)^2}\\&amp;=\frac{a(a-5)-1(a-5)}{(a+5)(a-5)} \\&amp; =\frac{(a-5)(a-1)}{(a+5)(a-5)}=\frac{a-1}{a+5}\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #153 (ID: 802040)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: রাজউক উত্তরা মডেল কলেজ, ঢাকা
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{6\left(x^2-6 x+5\right)}{8\left(x^2-25\right)}[/math] একটি বীজগাণিতিক ভগ্নাংশ।

ভগ্নাংশটির লব ও হরের গ.সা.গু. কত?

Options:
ক. [math]x - 5[/math]
খ. [math]2(x - 5)[/math]
গ. [math]2(x + 5)[/math]
ঘ. [math]2(x - 1)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \text { লব }=6\left(\mathrm{x}^2-6 \mathrm{x}+5\right)\\&amp;=3 \times 2\left(\mathrm{x}^2-5 \mathrm{x}-\mathrm{x}+5\right) \\ &amp;=3 \times 2\{\mathrm{x}(\mathrm{x}-5)-1(\mathrm{x}-5)\}\\&amp;=3 \times 2(\mathrm{x}-5) .(\mathrm{x}-1) \\ &amp; \text { হর }=8\left(\mathrm{x}^2-25\right)=2 \times 2 \times 2(\mathrm{x}+5)(\mathrm{x}-5) \\ &amp; \therefore \text { গ.সা.গু. }=2(\mathrm{x}-5)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #155 (ID: 802042)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^2+6 x+5}{x^2+10 x+25}[/math] এর সমতুল ভগ্নাংশ হবে-

i. [math]\frac{x+1}{x+5}[/math]

ii. [math]\frac{x^2-2 x-3}{x^2+2 x-15}[/math]

iii. [math]\frac{x^2+2 x+1}{x^2-3 x-10}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \frac{x^2+6 x+5}{x^2+10 x+25}=\frac{(x+1)(x+5)}{(x+5)(x+5)}=\frac{x+1}{x+5} \\&amp; \frac{x^2+2 x+1}{x^2-3 x-10}=\frac{x^2+2 \cdot x \cdot 1+1^2}{x^2-5 x+2 x-10} \\&amp; =\frac{(x+1)^2}{x(x-5)+2(x-5)}=\frac{(x+1)(x+1)}{(x+2)(x-5)}\end{aligned}[/math]সুতরাং (iii) নং তথ্যটি সঠিক নয়।

Explanation:

Question #168 (ID: 801912)

Question:

Question #171 (ID: 801915)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
i. [math]\frac{x}{y z} \div \frac{y}{z x}=\frac{x^2}{y^2}[/math]

ii. [math]\frac{z}{x y} \div \frac{x}{y z}=\frac{z^2}{x^2}[/math]

ক. i ও ii

Question #177 (ID: 801921)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x+3}{x^2+2 x+1}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{x^2-x-2}{x+3}[/math] দুইটি বীজগণিতীয় ভগ্নাংশ।

রাশি দুইটির গুণফল নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x+2}{x+1}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x+2}{x-1}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x-2}{x+1}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x-1}{x+2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{x^2-x-2}{x+3} \times \frac{x+3}{x^2+2 x+1}=\frac{x^2-2 x+x-2}{x+3} \times \frac{x+3}{x^2+2 \cdot x \cdot 1+1^2}[/math][math]\begin{aligned}=\frac{x(x-2)+1(x-2)}{(x+3)} \times \frac{(x+3)}{(x+1)^2} \\ =\frac{(x-2)(x+1)}{(x+3)} \times \frac{(x+3)}{(x+1)(x+1)}=\frac{x-2}{x+1}\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #178 (ID: 801922)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^3-y^3}{x^3+y^3} \div \frac{x^2+x y+y^2}{x^2-x y+y^2}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x-y}{x+y}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x+y}{x-y}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x-2y}{x+2y}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{y-x}{y+x}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \frac{x^3-y^3}{x^3+y^3} \div \frac{x^2+x y+y^2}{x^2-x y+y^2} \\ &amp; =\frac{(x-y)\left(x^2+x y+y^2\right)}{(x+y)\left(x^2-x y+y^2\right)} \times \frac{x^2-x y+y^2}{x^2+x y+y^2}\\&amp;=\frac{x-y}{x+y}\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #179 (ID: 801923)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}^3 \mathrm{b}^2}{\mathrm{c}^2 d} \div \frac{\mathrm{a}^2 \mathrm{b}^3}{\mathrm{c d}^3}=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{cd^2}{bc}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{bc}{ad^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{b^2c}{a^2d}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{ad^2}{bc}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{a^3 b^2}{c^2 d} \div \frac{a^2 b^3}{c^3}=\frac{a^3 b^2}{c^2 d} \times \frac{c d^3}{a^2 b^3}=\frac{a d^2}{b c}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #184 (ID: 801928)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যগুলো লক্ষ কর:

i. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{b}}+\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{b}}=\frac{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{b}}[/math]

ii. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{b}}+\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{d}}=\frac{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{bd}}[/math]

iii. [math]\frac{x}{a}+\frac{y}{b}+\frac{z}{c}=\frac{x b c+a c y+a b z}{a b c}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{b}}+\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{d}}=\frac{\mathrm{ad}}{\mathrm{bd}}+\frac{\mathrm{bc}}{\mathrm{bd}}=\frac{\mathrm{ad}+\mathrm{bc}}{\mathrm{bd}}[/math], সুতরাং উক্তিটি সঠিক নয়।

Explanation:

Question #189 (ID: 801933)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^2 y^3}{a^3 b^3} \times \frac{a^2 b^3}{x^3 y^3}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{ax}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a }{x}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{b}{x}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x}{b}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{x^2 y^3}{a^3 b^3} \times \frac{a^2 b^3}{x^3 y^3}=\frac{x^2 y^3 \cdot a^2 b^3}{x^2 y^3 a^2 b^3 \cdot a x}=\frac{1}{a x}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #203 (ID: 801947)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})^2}{\mathrm{a}^3+\mathrm{b}^3}[/math] দুইটি ভগ্নাংশ।

১ম ভগ্নাংশ থেকে ২য় ভগ্নাংশের বিয়োগফল কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a b}{a^3+b^3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{-a b}{a^3+b^3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a}{a^3+b^3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{-b}{a^3+b^3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{a+b}-\frac{(a-b)^2}{a^3+b^3}=\frac{1}{a+b}-\frac{(a-b)^2}{(a+b)\left(a^2-a b+b^2\right)}[math]=\frac{a^2-a b+b^2-(a-b)^2}{(a+b)\left(a^2-a b+b^2\right)}=\frac{a^2-a b+b^2-\left(a^2-2 a b+b^2\right)}{a^3+b^3}[/math]=\frac{a^2-a b+b^2-a^2+2 a b-b^2}{a^3+b^3}=\frac{a b}{a^3+b^3}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #204 (ID: 801948)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^2}{y z}, \frac{y^2}{z x}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{z^2}{x y}[/math] এর গুণফল নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x y z}{x^2 z^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x+y}{x z}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{xy }{x+y}[/math]
ঘ. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{x^2}{y z} \times \frac{y^2}{z x} \times \frac{z^2}{x y}=\frac{x^2 y^2 z^2}{x^2 y^2 z^2}=1[/math]

Question #207 (ID: 801951)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{(x-y)^2+4 x y}{x^2-y^2}, \frac{(x-y)^2}{x+y}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{(x+y)^2}{x-y}[/math] তিনটি বীজগণিতীয় রাশি।

১ম রাশি ২টির গুণফল কত?

Options:
ক. [math](x + y) [/math]
খ. [math](x - y) [/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x+y}{x-y}[/math]
ঘ. [math](x - y)(x - y) [/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{(x-y)^2+4 x y}{x^2-y^2} \times \frac{(x-y)^2}{x+y}=\frac{x+y}{x-y} \times \frac{(x-y)^2}{x+y}=x-y[/math]

Explanation:

Question #208 (ID: 801952)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{(x-y)^2+4 x y}{x^2-y^2}, \frac{(x-y)^2}{x+y}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{(x+y)^2}{x-y}[/math] তিনটি বীজগণিতীয় রাশি।

২য় ও ৩য় রাশির গুণফল কত?

Options:
ক. [math](x + y) [/math]
খ. [math]x ^ 2 + y ^ 2 [/math]
গ. [math]x ^ 2 - y ^ 2 [/math]
ঘ. [math]xy[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{(x-y)^2}{x+y} \times \frac{(x+y)^2}{x-y}=(x-y)(x+y)=x^2-y^2[/math]

Explanation:

Question #211 (ID: 801955)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
i. [math]\frac{x^2}{x^2-16} \div \frac{x}{x-4}=\frac{x}{x+4}[/math]

ii. [math]\frac{1}{x-2} \div \frac{2}{2-x}=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]

iii. [math]\frac{x}{x-4} \div \frac{x^2}{x-4}=\frac{1}{x^2}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
iii. [math]\frac{x}{x-4} \div \frac{x^2}{x-4}=\frac{x}{x-4} \times \frac{x-4}{x^2}=\frac{x}{x^2}=\frac{1}{x}[/math]; সুতরাং প্রদত্ত উক্তিটি সঠিক নয়।

Explanation:

Question #215 (ID: 801959)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: বি এ এফ শাহীন কলেজ, ঢাকা
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\mathrm{x}}{(\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y})^2}-\frac{\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}}{\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{y}^2}=[/math] ? 

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{y}{(x-y)^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{x}{(x+y)^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{x y}{(x+y)^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x}{(x-y)^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{x}{(x-y)^2}-\frac{x+y}{x^2-y^2}[/math][math]=\frac{x}{(x-y)(x-y)}-\frac{1}{(x-y)}=\frac{x-(x-y)}{(x-y)^2}=\frac{x-x+y}{(x-y)^2}=\frac{y}{(x-y)^2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #217 (ID: 801961)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{1-x+x^2}-\frac{1}{1+x+x^2}-\frac{2 x}{1+x^2+x^4}=\text { কত ? }[/math]

Options:
খ. 1
গ. [math] \frac{2 x}{1+x^2+x^4} [/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{1+x^2+x^4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \frac{1}{1-x+x^2}-\frac{1}{1+x+x^2}-\frac{2 x}{1+x^2+x^4} \\ &amp; =\frac{1+x+x^2-1+x-x^2}{\left(1-x+x^2\right)\left(1+x+x^2\right)}-\\&amp; \frac{2 x}{\left(1-x+x^2\right)\left(1+x+x^2\right)}=0\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #222 (ID: 801966)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ম. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1-x^2}{b+b^2} \times \frac{1-b^2}{1+x}=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{(1+x)(1-b)}{b}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{(1-x)(1+b)}{b}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{(1-x)(1-b)}{b}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{(1+x)(1+b)}{b}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1-x^2}{b+b^2} \times \frac{1-b^2}{1+x}=\frac{(1+x)(1-x)(1+b)(1-b)}{b(b+1)(1+x)}=\frac{(1-x)(1-b)}{b}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #231 (ID: 801975)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: চ. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y}}{\mathrm{xy}}+\frac{\mathrm{y}-\mathrm{z}}{\mathrm{yz}}+\frac{\mathrm{z}+\mathrm{x}}{\mathrm{zx}}=[/math] কত? 

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2 x}{y z}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2}{x y z}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\mathrm{z}}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2}{z}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math] \frac{x-y}{x y}+\frac{y-z}{y z}+\frac{z+x}{z x}[/math][math]=\frac{z x-y z+x y-z x+y z+x y}{x y z}=\frac{2 x y}{x y z}=\frac{2}{z}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #237 (ID: 801981)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm A=\frac{x+y}{x-y}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm B=\frac{x-y}{x+y}[/math] হলে- 

i. [math]\mathrm A[/math] ও [math]\mathrm B[/math] এর হরগুলোর ল.সা.গু [math]=x^2-y^2[/math]

ii. [math]\mathrm A-\mathrm B=\frac{2 x y}{x^2-y^2}[/math]

iii. [math]\mathrm A+\mathrm B=\frac{2\left(x^2+y^2\right)}{x^2-y^2}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যগুলো লক্ষ কর :

i. [math]\frac{x^3 y-x y^3}{x^2 y-x y^2}[/math] এর লঘিষ্ঠ রূপ হলো [math](x+y)[/math]

iii. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}}-\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}}[/math] এর সরলমান [math]=\frac{\mathrm{a}^2+\mathrm{b}^2}{\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{b}^2}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii

Question #247 (ID: 801991)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: চ. বো.'২০১৬;কু. বো.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{a}{a+b}+\frac{a b}{a^2-b^2}[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি? 

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a b}{a^2-b^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a^2 b}{a^2-b^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a+a b}{a^2-b^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{a^2}{a^2-b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{a}{a+b}+\frac{a b}{a^2-b^2}=\frac{a}{a+b}+\frac{a b}{(a+b)(a-b)}[/math][math]=\frac{a^2-a b+a b}{(a+b)(a-b)}=\frac{a^2}{a^2-b^2}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #255 (ID: 801999)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: কু. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{3 \mathrm{x}^2}{2 \mathrm{a}} \div \frac{4 \mathrm{y}^2}{15 \mathrm{xx}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{45 z x^3}{8 a y^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{45 \mathrm{zx}^3}{8 \mathrm{ay}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2 x y^2}{5 a z}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2 x y}{5 a z^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]8 \frac{3 x^2}{2 a} \div \frac{4 y^2}{15 z x}=\frac{3 x^2}{2 a} \times \frac{15 z x}{4 y^2}=\frac{45 z x^3}{8 a y^2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #258 (ID: 802002)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(\frac{x}{y}+\frac{y}{x}-1\right) \div\left(\frac{x^2}{y^2}-\frac{x}{y}+1\right)[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{x}{y}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\mathrm{y}}{\mathrm{x}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{y^2}{x}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2}{x}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\left(\frac{x}{y}+\frac{y}{x}-1\right) \div\left(\frac{x^2}{y^2}-\frac{x}{y}+1\right)\\=\frac{x^2+y^2-x y}{x y} \div \frac{x^2-x y+y^2}{y^2}[/math][math]=\frac{{x}^2+y^2-x y}{x y} \times \frac{y^2}{x^2-x y+y^2}=\frac{y^2}{x y}=\frac{y}{x}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #260 (ID: 802004)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ব. বো.'২০১৬;রা. বো.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{(a+b)^2-4 a b}{a^2+a b+b^2} \div \frac{1}{a^3-b^3}=[/math] কত? 

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}[/math]
খ. [math](\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})^2[/math]
গ. [math](\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})^3[/math]
ঘ. [math]a^2+a b+b^2[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \frac{(a+b)^2-4 a b}{a^2+a b+b^2} \div \frac{1}{a^3-b^3} \\&amp; =\frac{(a-b)^2}{\left(a^2+a b+b^2\right)} \times \frac{(a-b)\left(a^2+a b+b^2\right)}{1}\\&amp;=(a-b)^3\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #261 (ID: 802005)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ব. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}^2+2 \mathrm{a}+1}{\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{2 a}+\mathrm{1}} \div \frac{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{1}}{\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{1}}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি? 

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a+1}{a^2-1}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a^2-1}{a+1}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a-1}{a+1}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{a+1}{a-1}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{a^2+2 a+1}{a^2-2 a+1} \div \frac{a+1}{a-1}=\frac{(a+1)^2}{(a-1)^2} \times \frac{(a-1)}{(a+1)}=\frac{a+1}{a-1}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #266 (ID: 802010)

Question #271 (ID: 802015)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: রাজউক উত্তরা মডেল কলেজ, ঢাকা
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{a+b}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{1}{a-b}[/math] এর যোগফল থেকে কত বিয়োগ করলে বিয়োগফল 1 হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2}{a^2-b^2}-1[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2 a}{a^2-b^2}-1[/math]
গ. [math]1-\frac{2}{a^2-b^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]1-\frac{2 a}{a^2-b^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \frac{1}{a+b}+\frac{1}{a-b}-k=1 \\&amp; \text { হলে, } k=\frac{1}{a+b}+\frac{1}{a-b}-1 \\&amp; =\frac{a-b+a+b}{a^2-b^2}-1=\frac{2 a}{a^2-b^2}-1\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #272 (ID: 802016)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x^2+x-12}{x^2+2 x-15}[/math] একটি বীজগাণিতিক ভগ্নাংশ

কত থেকে ভগ্নাংশটির লঘিষ্ঠ মান বিয়োগ করলে বিয়োগফল [math]\frac{1}{x+5}[/math] হবে? 

Options:
ক. [math]-1[/math]
খ. [math]1[/math]
গ. [math]x + 4[/math]
ঘ. [math]x + 5[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; z-\frac{(x-3)(x+4)}{x^2+5 x-3 x-15}=\frac{1}{x+5} \\ &amp; \text { বা, } z=\frac{1}{x+5}+\frac{(x-3)(x+4)}{(x+5)(x-3)}\\&amp;=\frac{1}{x+5}+\frac{x+4}{x+5} \\ &amp; \quad=\frac{1+x+4}{x+5}=\frac{x+5}{x+5} \\ &amp; \therefore z=1\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #276 (ID: 802020)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ম. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(\frac{1}{2 x}+\frac{1}{y}\right) \div\left(\frac{1}{y}-\frac{1}{2 x}\right)[/math] এর সরল মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{(2 x+y)^2}{4 x y}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{4 x^2-y^2}{4 x^2 y^2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2 x+y}{2 x-y}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{(2 x+y)^2}{4 x^2 y^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \left(\frac{1}{2 x}+\frac{1}{y}\right) \div\left(\frac{1}{y}-\frac{1}{2 x}\right) \\&amp; =\frac{y+2 x}{2 x y} \div \frac{2 x-y}{2 x y}\\&amp;=\frac{(y+2 x)}{2 x y} \times \frac{2 x y}{2 x-y}=\frac{2 x+y}{2 x-y}\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #290 (ID: 801880)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{x+y}{x-y}[/math] ও [math]\frac{x-y}{x+y}[/math] কে সাধারণ হর বিশিষ্ট ভগ্নাংশে প্রকাশ করলে নিচের কোনটি হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{(x+y)^2}{x^2-y^2}, \frac{(x-y)^2}{x^2-y^2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{(x+y)^2}{x-y}, \frac{(x-y)^2}{x+y}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{(x+y)^2}{x^2+y^2}, \frac{(x-y)^2}{x^2+y^2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{x-y}{(x+y)^2}, \frac{x+y}{(x-y)^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
ভগ্নাংশ দুইটির হর [math](\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y})[/math] ও [math](\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y})[/math]এদের ল. সা. গু. [math]=(x+y)(x-y)[/math]১ম ভগ্নাংশ [math]=\frac{x+y}{x-y}=\frac{(x+y) \times(x+y)}{(x-y) \times(x+y)}=\frac{(x+y)^2}{x^2-y^2}[/math]২য় ভগ্নাংশ [math]=\frac{\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y}}{\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}}=\frac{(\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y}) \times(\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y})}{(\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}) \times(\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y})}=\frac{(\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y})^2}{\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{y}^2}[/math]

Explanation:
